2004-01-30: rcave@rcave01.schwabfoundation.org: ChangeSet 1.1873.1.2
  Previously, if an exception was set during an upgrade, the exceptionwas overwritten by the FUNCTION_FAILED execption.  This makes itimpossible to tell why an upgrade fails.  So check for an exceptionand return if an exception is already set.
  	* html/modules/modules/xaradminapi/executeinitfunction.php:
	  Check for current error type.  If there is an exception, then justreturn so that the exception is not overwritten by the functionfailed exceptions later in the code.
